				limit = {
					check_variable = { UKR_industrial_score < 50 }

				limit = {

			}

				limit = {

						radical_socialist = UKR_new_radsoc
						social_democrat = UKR_new_socdem
						social_liberal = party_popularity_100@social_liberal
						market_liberal = party_popularity_100@market_liberal
						social_conservative = party_popularity_100@social_conservative
						authoritarian_democrat = party_popularity_100@authoritarian_democrat
						paternal_autocrat = party_popularity_100@paternal_autocrat
						national_populist = party_popularity_100@national_populist
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_idea = UKR_minority_government
					}
					add_popularity = {
						ideology = syndicalist
						popularity = -0.025
					}
					add_popularity = {
						ideology = radical_socialist
						popularity = -0.025
					}
					add_popularity = {
						ideology = totalist
						popularity = -0.025
					}
				}
				else = {
					set_temp_variable = { UKR_urdp_attitude_change = 2 }
					UKR_urdp_relationship_improve = yes

					#Every additional idealism point adds an extra 25 political power
					set_temp_variable = { UKR_political_power_change = UKR_usdrp_idealism_points }
					clamp_temp_variable = { var = UKR_political_power_change min = 0 max = 4 }
					add_to_temp_variable = { UKR_political_power_change = 1 }
					multiply_temp_variable = { UKR_political_power_change = 25 }

					add_political_power = UKR_political_power_change
					add_popularity = {
						ideology = syndicalist
						popularity = -0.025
					}
					add_popularity = {
						ideology = radical_socialist
						popularity = -0.025
					}
					add_popularity = {
						ideology = totalist
						popularity = -0.025
					}
					custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
					country_event = ukraine_republican_events.150
					custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
					UKR_idealism_spend = yes
					custom_effect_tooltip = UKR_for_every_level_of_idealism_we_will_gain
					effect_tooltip = { add_political_power = 25 }
				}
			}
		}
